<h1 _ngcontent-wmo-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="应用UI测试（基于Python）"> 应用UI测试（基于Python） </h1>

<div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted" style="position: relative;"> <div id="body0000001822901865"><div class="tiledSection"><h2 id="section16890204264419">框架概述<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section16890204264419" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p861863602010">DevEco Testing Hypium （以下简称Hypium）是HarmonyOS平台的UI自动化测试框架，支持用户使用Python语言为应用编写UI自动化测试脚本，主要包含以下特性：</p> <ol id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ol1861893615208"><li id="li9618113619206">Hypium提供了控件、图像和比例坐标等<strong>多种控件定位能力</strong>，支持多窗口操作以及触摸屏/鼠标/键盘等<strong>多种模拟输入功能</strong>，支持<strong>多设备</strong>并行操作，能够覆盖各类场景和多种形态设备上的自动化用例编写需求，可支持鸿蒙手机、平板、PC等设备。</li><li id="li1861813620209">Hypium提供了在PyCharm中使用的<strong>用例编写辅助插件</strong>，支持控件查看/投屏操作等多种用例开发辅助功能，提升用例开发体验和效率。</li><li id="li261811363206">Hypium能够为执行的用例生成详细的<strong>用例执行报告</strong>，并且自动记录设备日志以及执行步骤截图，为用户提供高效和专业的测试用例执行和结果分析体验。</li></ol> </div> <div class="tiledSection"><h2 id="section191615399595">安装向导<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section191615399595" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18626165084713"><strong>1.安装Python</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p377316249474">推荐从<a href="https://www.python.org/" target="_blank">Python官网</a>安装Python3.10版本。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p23826377472"><strong>2.安装PyCharm</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3361114591713">推荐从<a href="https://www.jetbrains.com.cn/en-us/pycharm/" target="_blank">PyCharm官网</a>安装2022.3以后的社区版本。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p164071147567">项目创建功能只支持2022.3至2025.1的Pycharm版本。2024.3版本由于pycharm自身原因，只能选择单设备模板进行创建。</p> </div></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11377157101817"><strong>3.安装hdc</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12161314737">请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc" target="_blank">调试工具-hdc</a>中环境准备章节来安装和配置hdc环境。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p663903133910"><strong>4.安装</strong><strong>Hypium</strong></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul971355712593"><li id="li14713175713593"><strong>方式一：</strong><strong>PyPI在线安装(推荐)</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18892512113">在命令行中执行以下命令安装最新版本hypium</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-undefined" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen9932510216" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>pip install hypium -U</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12581312417"></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul62891181218"><li id="li82899189115"><strong>方式二：安装包离线安装</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11225274115">访问华为开发者联盟官网<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/download/deveco-testing-hypium" target="_blank">下载DevEco Testing Hypium安装包</a>。下载后解压该安装包，找到其中的hypium-6.0.6.210.zip（此版本仅作为示例，请以实际版本号为准）。再次解压hypium-6.0.6.210.zip，进入解压后的文件目录执行以下命令，按照顺序安装4个安装包（命令中版本号仅做示例，请以实际版本号为准）。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-bash" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen19155654131913" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>python -m pip install xdevice-6.0.6.210.tar.gz</li><li>python -m pip install xdevice-devicetest-6.0.6.210.tar.gz</li><li>python -m pip install xdevice-ohos-6.0.6.210.tar.gz</li><li>python -m pip install hypium-6.0.6.210.tar.gz</li><li>
</li><li><span class=""><span class="hljs-comment"># </span></span><span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">此版本仅作为示例，实际请根据项目使用的版本选择</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p16301371020"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p103171494201"><strong>5.DevEco Testing Hypium插件安装及使用方法</strong></p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p19760152813319">Mac系统使用UiViewer功能时，需在设置面板中手动指定hdc路径，详情可见 <strong>本小节中 · 插件功能 Ⅳ.设置面板区域-hdc路径</strong>。</p> </div></div></div> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul7310192514811"><li id="li1531042514483"><strong>插件安装</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p75841959183919">Ⅰ. 访问华为开发者联盟官网<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/download/deveco-testing-hypium" target="_blank">下载页面</a>下载DevEco Testing Hypium安装包，下载后解压该安装包，找到其中的hypium-pycharm-plugin-6.0.6.210.zip（该版本号仅做示例，请以实际版本号为准），此文件为插件的安装包，无需再进行解压。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p158251835104815"><span><img originheight="598" originwidth="1010" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201405.50017809029220841853682943944410:50001231000000:2800:0F40F90BE0EDA9E7CF0E35AA95F2B0CC7B28477C7EC4E732292BB9223BF76A71.jpg" title="点击放大" width="920" height="544.7128712871287"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p25169399482">Ⅱ. 打开PyCharm后，点击File -&gt; Settings -&gt; Plugin -&gt; 齿轮图标 -&gt; Install Plugin from Disk。在弹出的文件选择器中，选择第一步下载的hypium-pycharm-plugin-6.0.6.210.zip（该版本号仅做示例，请以实际版本号为准）离线安装包，完成安装。安装完成后，重启PyCharm即可使用新安装的DevecoTesting Hypium插件。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1994605320395"><span><img originheight="318" originwidth="1013" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201405.79018542235005810953611640047586:50001231000000:2800:FDA91109BDDC2EF2A6AA2872E4775C2E6C4759646A1E26B372D755E1F2712175.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="288.8055281342547"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p204304386274">安装完成后在Plugins界面可以看到DevEcoTesting-Hypium插件。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p312719713395"><span><img originheight="721" originwidth="984" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201405.53227865896386394748847824341408:50001231000000:2800:10644B567D8869AD3AD1F578CDF86B2AB7955FF30529BE03B58A300DE8BDD76F.png" width="920" height="674.1056910569106"></span></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul193341224919"><li id="li11933101274916"><strong>插件功能</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p153773215469">PyCharm有三个主要的开发功能区，如下图所示。DevEco Testing Hypium插件在不同的开发功能区提供了对应的用例开发辅助功能，在PyCharm的设置面板中提供了插件的设置功能，在PyCharm的工程新建面板中提供了用例工程模板创建功能，下文分区域介绍这些功能。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p050171318412"><span><img originheight="608" originwidth="1436" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201406.12374351644313895426381003228709:50001231000000:2800:C303E6E26BECDA4B78DD799F15628923396920F78073E7465F824A6161631444.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="389.52646239554315"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5423324134919"><strong>Ⅰ. 项目文件区域</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p372412614419">在项目文件区域右键点击项目目录或者文件，选择 DevEco Testing Hypium，弹出对应的功能菜单。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12298273414"><span><img originheight="254" originwidth="638" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201406.61545505152547531761235195599060:50001231000000:2800:5C2441F30A51B4A512966421FF088DEF35B38BB1E90FF6AE41C20E80855D6BD1.png" width="638" height="254"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p186411636134415">功能菜单根据选择的目录和文件不同存在区别，详细参见下表：</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ol983020219452"><li id="li9831192116450">该功能仅在右键点击项目根目录时可用，选中其他目录无法触发此功能。</li><li id="li15830133554510">项目根目录下需要包含 testcases 文件夹。</li><li id="li1831102120453">项目根目录下需存在 setup-sceneperf.py 或 setup-regression.py 文件之一，以支持相应测试服务包的生成。</li></ol> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3512238504"><strong>Ⅱ. 代码编辑区域</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table15636152892212" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row12780728132216"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.36.1.6.1.1" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p16406124792210">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.36.1.6.1.2" valign="top" width="18.05%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p8780162852212">功能</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.36.1.6.1.3" valign="top" width="39.910000000000004%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1278022842215">图片</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.36.1.6.1.4" valign="top" width="11.4%"><p </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p888507115020"><strong>Ⅲ. ToolWindow区域</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p41611773318"><strong>UiViewer功能</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p716977339">DevEco Testing Hypium插件会在PyCharm界面右边缘的ToolWindow区域生成UiViewer标签，点击后会展开UiViewer功能面板。UiViewer功能目前分为4个界面：设备选择界面 、单设备控件查看界面 、单设备投屏界面 、双设备投屏界面。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1244951443213">UiViewer插件当前仅支持USB连接本地设备调测，暂不支持模拟器。</p> </div></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p171573423518"><strong>设备选择界面</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p171657123311">设备选择界面如下图所示， 若首次进入该界面，或设备状态发生变化，需点击“刷新”按钮以更新设备列表。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13614813711"><span><img originheight="497" originwidth="499" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201406.62115431248717290831105159588832:50001231000000:2800:C5E82E44EABBD046F50DE52F5CDC9DC67443196543E68E2820960C8DA5FBA129.png" title="点击放大" width="499" height="497"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p14226134455319">设备信息说明见下表：</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table9983119375" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row114483116374"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.45.1.4.1.1" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p78561035173713">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.45.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="15.76%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p21445312378">参数名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.45.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="76.72%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p111441831163712">说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row31441631173713"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1085611353372">1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.76%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p314453114371">SN（Serial Number）号</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="76.72%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18144133123719">该参数为已连接设备的序列号（SN号），用于区分不同设备。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row81441931153717"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5856143533713">2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.76%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1814433110374">设备类型</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="76.72%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18107832132113">该参数为设备连接通道类型，仅支持hdc连接，对应设备类型显示为HDC。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1814543115377"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p208561235183718">3</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.76%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1714510315379">设备状态</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="76.72%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9145143117377">该参数显示当前设备是否支持使用 UiViewer 工具：“OK” 表示该设备可用；“NOT_SUPPORT” 表示设备不可用。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row151451231153718"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18856173593715">4</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.76%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1814511313371">设备编号</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="76.72%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p240141917582">该参数用于在多设备同时投屏时配置各设备的显示位置，用户可手动进行调整。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p440191925815">在双设备投屏界面中，默认情况下，设备编号为 dev1 的设备显示在左侧，设备编号为 dev2 的设备显示在右侧。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p82401332175419">设备选择界面最多支持同时选择两个设备进行投屏。</p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul1169719334"><li id="li1279113615017">若仅勾选一个设备并点击“确定”按钮，则进入单设备投屏界面。</li><li id="li1120415490438">若勾选了两个设备并点击“确定”按钮，将进入双设备投屏界面；其中，设备编号为 “dev1” 的设备显示在左侧，设备编号为 “dev2”的设备显示在右侧，用户可以通过设备编号的下拉选项框自定义配置设备编号，控制双设备投屏。</li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5831192013512"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p7803171613380"><strong>单设备投屏界面</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9805124316192"><span><img originheight="866" originwidth="595" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201406.10233271932078310966747122081375:50001231000000:2800:38582B83D6F047862E915BDAA589105EABE43DA5E2484DB4C781D91DD5BCC34C.png" title="点击放大" width="595" height="866"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p552965119404"><strong>功能说明：</strong></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul14529185184019"><li id="li109851339598"><strong>设备切换按钮：</strong>点击后返回设备选择界面，可重新选择要投屏的设备。</li><li id="li19529251194012"><strong>设备屏幕显示区域：</strong>显示当前设备的实时屏幕画面。在投屏模式下，可通过鼠标点击或滑动该界面来操作设备。</li><li id="li1052925164018"><strong>工具区：</strong>位于设备屏幕显示区域右侧，从上至下分为以下三个子工具区。</li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p15529195184017"><strong>工具区1：</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1852955144019">该工具区提供控件查看功能。进入控件查看模式后，设备画面将保持静止，不再实时更新。若需获取当前页面的最新控件信息，需手动点击“控件刷新”按钮以重新抓取页面结构和控件数据。</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table1751853314114" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row16659193313419"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.55.1.5.1.1" valign="top" width="7.519248075192481%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p19448181964610">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.55.1.5.1.2" valign="top" width="20.007999200079993%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13659113319412">图标</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.55.1.5.1.3" valign="top" width="18.36816318368163%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17659123313417">功能</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.55.1.5.1.4" valign="top" width="54.1045895410459%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p8659133194113">说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row15659033194112"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.519248075192481%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p34481219184613">1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20.007999200079993%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p128828101558"><span><img originheight="72" originwidth="72" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201406.94624995896660926839676001824549:50001231000000:2800:48AD6633E0C041A928153CCC869B9A14C43D13E88CAC9D0719AE8339B9AFD807.jpg" class="notEnlarge" width="72" height="72"></span></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="18.36816318368163%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p116591133134110">查看控件</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="54.1045895410459%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p577810423314">点击该按钮进入控件查看模式，插件会读取设备当前的控件树和屏幕截图，并显示到界面上（此过程需要一定时间，在鼠标光标处于转圈状态时，请勿点击其他按钮，以免操作冲突或导致异常）。在控件查看模式下再次点击该按钮，可退出当前模式，返回实时投屏模式。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1165973310419"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.519248075192481%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p104481219154616">2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20.007999200079993%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p125267301456"><span><img originheight="72" originwidth="72" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201406.93546521501796988340171563984554:50001231000000:2800:E465654B16CFA948B19099520039792DA9BD35C4253062FD2FDEB080D83D4014.jpg" class="notEnlarge" width="72" height="72"></span></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="18.36816318368163%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1165953315417">进入高级控件查看模式</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="54.1045895410459%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p550017466618">点击该按钮进入高级控件查看模式，系统会根据鼠标移动实时高亮对应控件，并持续展示其控件信息。点击某一控件信息后，将自动切换到普通控件查看模式，并定位显示该控件在控件树中的详细信息。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12500164614616">处于高级控件查看模式时，再次点击该按钮，可退出当前模式，则返回实时投屏模式。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1565963312416"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.519248075192481%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18448131919464">3</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20.007999200079993%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p137312491684"><span><img originheight="72" originwidth="72" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201406.28137906700037723895050956179400:50001231000000:2800:98E23E33AF59616631D21DAE9B2F4395FC87BAF3A7C2FB44F4385A6347EFF16D.png" class="notEnlarge" width="72" height="72"></span></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="18.36816318368163%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p48531293109">录制Hypium测试用例脚本</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="54.1045895410459%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17716122109">点击该按钮进入操作录制模式，在此模式下，用户点击或操作投屏画面中的控件时，系统将自动识别操作行为，并在编辑器当前光标位置生成对应的 Hypium 自动化测试脚本代码。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1277201231011">处于操作录制模式时，再次点击该按钮可退出当前模式，返回实时投屏模式。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row166193313414"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.519248075192481%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11448101964610">4</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20.007999200079993%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row11424739142916"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.519248075192481%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p661057132919">9</p> </td> <td src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201407.86849773507712882086225094872852:50001231000000:2800:8CCF3BEDCE66D5C700B38A88323BF3BFD2EE0F596C972063CECE389621BABA46.jpg" class="notEnlarge" width="72" height="72"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p411154912338"></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="18.36816318368163%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1442493920298">管理应用</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="54.17458254174582%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11420124441418">点击该按钮后将打开一个独立的应用管理界面，用户可以在应用管理界面安装和卸载应用。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row2083117461227"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.519248075192481%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6831124616229">10</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.938006199380062%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11832164672219"><span><img originheight="72" originwidth="72" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201407.87142205770271113630625786449500:50001231000000:2800:E08EDAE2EF3DC50E6CE55A4FA194B5E1319DD912B6D1D279F92C415F8E76F3B3.png" class="notEnlarge" width="72" height="72"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p54581543172417"></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="18.36816318368163%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p440817273248">录制文本输入</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="54.17458254174582%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1795511358244">此按钮在进入录制状态后才能够使用。点击此按钮后将进入录制输入状态，此时点击界面上要进行输入的文本框控件后，会弹出一个输出框；用户在输入框中输入要插入的文本后点击确定，此时工具便会在代码编辑区光标处生成录制出的文本输入语句，同时设备侧也会自动输入文本。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p15479205510335"><strong>双设备投屏界面</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p952864614151">该界面支持同时对两个设备进行投屏与操作，双设备投屏时，每个设备的显示区域功能与单设备投屏一致，支持独立触摸控制、截图、旋转等操作。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p55286463159">当需要对某一设备进行控件查看时，插件将自动退出双设备投屏模式，切换至单设备控件查看界面，以确保控件信息的准确展示与操作体验。完成控件查看后，用户可手动返回双设备投屏视图。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p36024377314"><span><img originheight="866" originwidth="1065" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201407.07581835520526338202564736642344:50001231000000:2800:49DE3020CC346A106A34C3CCD44324ABD49A071A9C4D7604067E609FAAE470FD.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="748.0938967136151"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12465326352"><strong>执行结果报告展示功能</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p176371112203511">使用“一键执行当前用例”功能完成测试用例执行后，插件将在控制台旁边自动生成执行结果标签。点击该标签，即可查看本次用例执行过程中各步骤的截图。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p698216476522"><span><img originheight="387" originwidth="1819" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201407.34140818554796434666540206538650:50001231000000:2800:8C6C10E2D43B158EC0D234E5EA9C4F0A0C7216DDF3307B09921D6791E229B763.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="195.73391973611876"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1112315496361"><strong>Ⅳ. 设置面板区</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17166134203711">打开PyCharm设置面板，选中左侧的DevEco Testing Hypium选项，可以进入DevEco Testing Hypium的设置面板，如下图所示。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p917018497339"><span><img originheight="721" originwidth="984" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201408.46956873617881855487471893256672:50001231000000:2800:7EFC8789113EE3ACFE85264B874A3BDFA9A8251180B610EF309B8E9CA579C9F7.png" width="920" height="674.1056910569106"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p28421136112916">各个配置项的详细说明见下表：</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table1430815617403" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1530812616405"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.73.1.5.1.1" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13886210134312">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.73.1.5.1.2" valign="top" width="19.508049195080492%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p230816611407">功能</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.73.1.5.1.3" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1730810644016">说明</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.2.73.1.5.1.4" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1630896144019">注意</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row33083664019"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1730818618406">配置一键执行/调试功能所使用的配置文件路径，如不设置，默认使用当前项目下的config文件夹作为配置文件路径。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p430816114012">-</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row23081967407"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1930818614013">配置一键执行/调试功能所使用的测试文件路径，如不设置，则默认使用当前项目下的testcases文件夹作为测试用例路径。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1130836194013">-</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row11308166164012"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p68871107434">3</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.508049195080492%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1630810614404">额外执行参数</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p830815644014">配置运行用例一键执行/调试功能时，额外传递给Hypium测试框架的命令行参数。例如用户需要开启Hypium框架的用例单步骤截图功能，可以将额外执行参数设置为“-ta screenshot:true”。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p10273162053315">-</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row030917624017"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1887710134311">4</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.508049195080492%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1030946124015">是否以bin模式执行</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p830956124014">配置是否以bin模式执行用例时，通过该模式执行时，可避免投屏和用例执行冲突。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1674684124619"><strong>正常使用时该选项无需配置。</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1730917615407">该设置项在DevEco Testing Hypium 6.0.5.200以及更新的版本中不再需要，已移除。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row056716315373"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p8567133173720">5</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.508049195080492%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1256793183712">hdc路径</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p65673353710">配置UiViewer所使用的hdc路径。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p10567135371">-</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row830913614018"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p78877105438">6</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.508049195080492%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2309166194013">高级控件查看模式自动刷新间隔</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p4309156164013">配置UiViewer功能中的高级控件查看模式的刷新间隔，默认60秒自动重新获取一次界面的布局，最小时间可以设为30秒，最大时间300秒。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p43091467408">-</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1398881211613"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p89885120168">7</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.508049195080492%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p89898127161">录制步骤是否生成性能脚本</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1898961212160">操作录制模式默认生成功能测试脚本，通过该选项可以配置生成性能测试步骤脚本。注意执行性能测试脚本需要首先安装hypium-perf性能测试插件。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1298971217166">该功能仅DevEco Testing Hypium 6.0.5.200以及更新的版本支持。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1285601712389"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p148561617163820">8</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.508049195080492%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p19856617113811">是否使用视频流投屏模式</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p885671712383">配置是否使用视频流模式投屏。当投屏异常时，可尝试将此选项改为否，切换投屏方式，注意此时的投屏帧率大幅降低，</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5856151720386"><strong>正常使用时该选项无需进行配置。</strong></p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row532351044013"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p158875107433">9</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.508049195080492%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1732414101406">依赖下载参数</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2045515528418">配置生成测试服务包下载PyPI依赖包是传递给pip命令的额外参数。例如出现依赖下载慢或失败的情况时，可设置“-i &lt;PyPI Source&gt;”参数，配置可正常访问的PyPI源。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p632415107405">-</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row11805203691614"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.288871112888712%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p880503641618">10</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.508049195080492%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p8805163610165">本地依赖文件存放文件夹</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="42.17578242175782%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17805153617166">设置该文件夹后，在生成测试服务包时，插件将优先使用该目录中已下载的依赖文件，避免重复在线下载，有效应对因网络问题导致的PyPI依赖包安装失败等场景。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="27.02729727027297%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11805123631611">-</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p42191658537"><strong>Ⅴ. 工程创建区域</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1964534644310">在PyCharm顶部点击File -&gt; New Project 进入模板工程创建面板。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17704131644417"><span><img originheight="142" originwidth="402" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201408.70601960760747259199840907414656:50001231000000:2800:7C9A864EECBEED9B2406C986B3BE9F9957B641B509391085E3F27A4AD338D9E3.png" width="402" height="142"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p20628193523">点击左侧的DevEco Testing Hypium，可以创建Hypium用例模板工程。共有两种类型的Hypium模板工程，分别对应单设备和双设备的测试场景。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p10607644135712"><span><img originheight="648" originwidth="799" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201408.34905664195849182806055745779114:50001231000000:2800:21871D97B1F77298EBD85269A50CC1AA2D6AA5174105AB7BDC8322F1D3A234DC.jpg" title="点击放大" width="799" height="648"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p59917484342">选择对应模板，配置工程路径以及Python环境参数，点击Create即可创建Hypium测试用例工程。工程目录中包含一个模板用例和一个模板配置文件user_config.xml。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1548564010468">以单设备工程为例，创建完成后的界面如下图所示。连接被测设备后，可右键点击模板用例文件代码编辑区域“执行hypium用例”来运行当前用例。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p28266525243"><span><img originheight="750" originwidth="1575" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201408.83577085193401748189495583896501:50001231000000:2800:7131CB7A2B7D0E92BBC42A10294BE5F08342DDC5200492B9A4CF5285BC72B9CE.png" width="920" height="438.09523809523813"></span></p> </div> <div class="tiledSection"><h2 id="section589563925210">测试脚本开发快速入门<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section589563925210" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1531053195514">本章节将指导用户创建并执行一个简单的测试脚本工程，快速掌握项目目录结构中的关键文件，熟悉基于Hypium的测试脚本开发流程。</p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul489620394529"><li id="li138965396528"><strong>测试脚本工程创建</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3896939195214">测试脚本工程创建主要有两种方式：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p108961139145219">a）直接使用以下附件中的模板工程。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9896123919522"><a data-hd-attachment="true" href="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201409.75697659191060809151386814142127:50001231000000:2800:ADE23F1AAA8A021B240473886EAFB71696B0D00B61A73CD86433262511E31C90.zip?needInitFileName=true">HypiumProjectTemplate.zip</a></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p589693995214">b）通过PyCharm上的DevEcoTesting-Hypium插件进行创建。请参考本文档的<strong>“安装向导 -&gt; DevEco Testing Hypium插件安装及使用方法 -&gt; 插件功能 -&gt; 工程创建区域</strong><strong>”</strong>小节。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p118961398527"><strong>Ⅰ.工程目录文件介绍</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div class="hljs-name">screenshot</span>&gt;</span></li><li>        <span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- screenrecorder，用例Step步骤是否录屏。true开启/false不开启，默认值false --&gt;</span></li><li>        <span id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p189983955211"><strong>Ⅲ.测试用例介绍</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6319162445212">Hypium 测试用例由两部分组成：测试用例配置文件（JSON 格式）和测试用例脚本文件（Python 格式）。测试用例的组织方式支持两种模式：</p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul6319224135210"><li id="li15319192413525"><strong>单个用例模式：</strong>包含一个测试用例脚本（Python）文件和一个测试用例配置（JSON）文件；</li><li id="li9983173112535"><strong>测试套模式：</strong>包含一个测试套脚本（Python）文件、多个测试用例脚本（Python）文件和一个测试套配置（JSON）文件。</li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p14639759125316">用户可根据实际需求选择合适的组织方式。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p05081052135310"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p189002398524"><strong>单个测试用例模式</strong></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul925573013113"><li id="li172557305113"><strong>测试用例脚本文件</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p16795335175517">该文件包含测试用例的执行逻辑，核心为三个关键的生命周期函数：setup、process、teardown。在用例开发时，用户需要根据业务需求在对应的函数中编写测试逻辑代码。生命周期函数的详细说明见下表：</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table179005399524" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row169001639135219"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.20.1.4.1.1" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p090023910523">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.20.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="17.45%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5900339185219">生命周期函数</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.20.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="75.03%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p10900123917528">说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1790183915218"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p49011839185213">1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="17.45%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2901839155213">setup</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="75.03%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p14901439135214">测试用例的前置步骤，主要用于执行测试用例的预置动作。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row16901439185213"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1901103905210">2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="17.45%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1690183918529">process</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="75.03%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13901173945217">测试用例的实际操作步骤，主要描述当前测试用例中的所有测试用例步骤集合。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row16901039185218"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p139012039185219">3</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="17.45%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p79021639195212">teardown</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="75.03%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6902133935214">测试用例的清理步骤，主要用于执行测试用例的环境清理等操作。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p46594010585"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-python" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen1390223955210" data-highlighted="yes"><ol devicetest.core.test_case <strong><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></strong> TestCase, Step</li><li><strong><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></strong> devicetest.utils.file_util class="hljs-keyword">import</span></strong> *</li><li><strong><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></strong> aw <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> Utils</li><li><strong><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <strong><span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">__init__</span></span></strong>(<span class="hljs-params">self, controllers</span>):</li><li>        self.TAG = self.__class__.__name__</li><li>        TestCase.__init__(self, self.TAG, controllers)</li><li>        self.driver = UiDriver(self.device1)</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <strong><span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">setup</span></span></strong>(<span class="hljs-params">self</span>):</li><li>        Step(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">'1.回到桌面'</span></span>)</li><li>        self.driver.swipe_to_home()</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <strong><span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">process</span></span></strong>(<span class="hljs-params">self</span>):</li><li>        Step(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">'2.检查短信应用版本'</span></span>)</li><li>        mms_version = Utils.get_app_version_code(self.driver, <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">'com.ohos.mms'</span></span>)</li><li>        host.check_greater(mms_version, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)</li><li>        Step(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">'3.点击桌面上的短信'</span></span>)</li><li>        self.driver.touch(BY.text(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"信息"</span></span>))</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <strong><span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">teardown</span></span></strong>(<span class="hljs-params">self</span>):</li><li>        Step(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"4. 停止短信应用"</span></span>)</li><li>        self.driver.stop_app(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"com.ohos.mms"</span></span>)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p205698480588"></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul4563336918"><li id="li1556318361114"><strong>测试用例配置文件</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9906203925213">该文件主要描述测试用例的配置信息，如测试用例所需设备类型和数量、测试用例的测试驱动信息、测试用例的描述信息等。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p20742029182912"><strong>注意</strong>：JSON文件不支持注释，请在使用示例时移除其中以 “//”开头的注释部分。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2439113716320"><strong>示例：</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cangjie" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen990603995211" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>{</li><li>    <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// description属性为测试用例的功能描述。</span></span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-string">"description"</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"Config for app test suites"</span></span>,</li><li>    <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// environment属性用于配置测试用例需要的设备类型和数量。</span></span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-string">"environment"</span>: [</li><li>        {</li><li>            <span class="hljs-string">"type"</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"device"</span></span>,   <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// 设备操作系统类型，device表示HarmonyOS设备</span></span><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>            <span class="hljs-string">"label"</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"phone"</span></span>   <span class=""> <span class="hljs-comment">// 设备物理形态，phone为手机，tablet为平板，设置为空字符串或者移除该属性表示用例对设备类型无要求。用户可以通过执行hdc shell param get const.product.devicetype查看设备类型。</span></span></li><li>        }，</li><li>        {</li><li>            <span class="hljs-string">"type"</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"device"</span></span>,   <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// 测试用例需要多个设备时，在environment属性中添加多个设备配置项。</span></span></li><li>            <span class="hljs-string">"label"</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"phone"</span></span></li><li>        }</li><li>    ],</li><li>    <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// driver字段主要描述测试用例的测试驱动是什么，以及具体要执行的Python脚本文件在哪（填写与当前JSON文件的相对路径即可）</span></span></li><li><span class="">    <span class="hljs-comment">// 不填写则在当前JSON文件下寻找同名Python文件</span></span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-string">"driver"</span>: {</li><li>        <span class="hljs-string">"type"</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"DeviceTest"</span></span>,</li><li>           }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p490818394527"><strong>测试套模式</strong></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul7556173971814"><li id="li155618395185"><strong>测试套脚本文件</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1562019587189">该文件包含测试套的初始化和清理逻辑，核心为两个关键的生命周期函数：setup、teardown。在用例开发时，用户需要根据业务需求在对应的函数中编写测试逻辑代码。生命周期函数的详细说明见下表：</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table199081939175213" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row69089391523"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.32.1.4.1.1" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13908039185215">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.32.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="46.239999999999995%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p189081439175210">生命周期函数</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.32.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="46.239999999999995%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p20908133955213">说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row49098397527"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2909123911529">1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="46.239999999999995%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p690953925217">setup</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="46.239999999999995%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1790923916528">整个测试套的前置步骤，在测试套运行前先执行该函数。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1890912391529"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p179091439105215">2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="46.239999999999995%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p390917398523">teardown</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="46.239999999999995%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18909183919520">整个测试套的清理步骤，在执行完所有测试用例后执行。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1452415548191"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-python" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen109101139185211" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="hljs-comment"># 测试套的前置步骤将在所有测试用例执行前运行。当多个测试用例具有相同的初始化操作时，可将共用的前置逻辑定义在此。</span></span></li><li>   <strong> <span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></strong> <strong><span class=""><span setup"</span></span>)</li><li>    <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment"># 测试套的清理步骤会在所有测试用例执行完成后运行。</span></span></li><li>   <strong> <span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> </strong><strong><span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">teardown</span></span></strong>(<span class="hljs-params">self</span>):</li><li>        Step(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"TestSuite: teardown"</span></span>)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul1254374208"><li id="li202545711201"><strong>测试套配置文件</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p15334519207">该文件主要描述测试套的配置信息，如测试套所需设备类型和数量、测试套的测试驱动信息、测试套的描述信息等。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p111451510132316"><strong>注意</strong>：JSON文件不支持注释，请在使用示例时移除其中以 “//”开头的注释部分。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17461158212"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cangjie" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen129111139205211" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>{</li><li>    <span class="hljs-string">"description"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"</span><span class=""><span class="hljs-string">Config for app test suites</span></span><span class="hljs-string">"</span>,</li><li><span class="">    <span class="hljs-comment">// environment属性用于配置测试用例需要的设备类型和数量。</span></span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-string">"environment"</span>: [</li><li>        {</li><li>            <span class="hljs-string">"type"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"</span><span class=""><span class="hljs-string">device</span></span><span class="hljs-string">"</span>,     <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// 配置设备操作系统类型，device表示HarmonyOS设备</span></span><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>            <span class="hljs-string">"label"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"</span><span class=""><span class="hljs-string">phone</span></span><span class="hljs-string">"</span>      <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// 设备物理形态，phone为手机，tablet为平板，设置为空字符串或者移除该属性表示用例对设备类型无要求。用户可以通过执行hdc shell param get const.product.devicetype查看设备类型。</span></span></li><li>        }</li><li>    ],</li><li>    <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// driver 属性用于定义测试用例的驱动类型及待执行脚本的路径，脚本路径需为相对于当前 JSON 文件的路径</span></span><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-string">"driver"</span>: {</li><li>        <span class="hljs-string">"type"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"</span><span class=""><span class="hljs-string">DeviceTestSuite</span></span><span class="hljs-string">"</span>,</li><li><span class="">        <span class="hljs-comment">// 指定测试套配置（JSON）文件对应的测试套脚本（Python）文件路径（可省略 .py 后缀），支持相对路径或绝对路径。若使用相对路径，需相对于测试工程根目录；若未指定，则默认查找与当前 JSON 文件同目录下同名的 Python文件。</span></span></li><li>        <span class="hljs-string">"testsuite"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"</span><span class=""><span class="hljs-string">TS_001/TS_001</span></span><span class="hljs-string">"</span>,</li><li><span class="">        <span class="hljs-comment">// 指定测试套中的测试用例脚本(Python)文件列表，指定方式有两种。</span></span></li><li><span class="">        <span class="hljs-comment">// 方式一：定义 suitecases 字段，并在其中指定测试用例脚本文件的路径。路径可使用相对路径或绝对路径；若使用相对路径，其根目录为当前测试套目录。</span></span></li><li>        <span class="hljs-string">"suitecases"</span>: [</li><li>            <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"TestCase1.py"</span>,         </span><span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// 相对路径</span></span></li><li><span class="">            <span class="hljs-string">"/path/to/TestCase2.py"</span></span> <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// 绝对路径</span></span></li><li>        ]</li><li>        <span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">// 方式二：将测试用例脚本（Python）文件保存到测试套目录中，并且设置文件名前缀为"TC_"，框架即可自动扫描当前测试套对应的所有测试用例脚本文件。</span></span></li><li>    },</li><li><span class="">    <span class="hljs-comment">// kits字段主要描述测试用例需要的测试公共kit，如pushkit、shellkit等</span></span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-string">"kits"</span>: []</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul1414642605011"><li id="li4146326185012"><strong>测试用例脚本文件</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1913539165211">测试套模式中的测试用例脚本文件和单个测试用例中对应文件完全相同，请参考上文<strong>“单个测试用例模式</strong> -&gt; <strong>测试用例脚本文件</strong>“小节。此处介绍测试用例脚本文件和测试套关联的两种方式：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2914133913521"><strong>方式一：</strong>框架自动扫描的与测试套关联的测试用例脚本，测试用例脚本的保存目录和文件命名需要满足以下规则：</p> <ol id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ol1033293735010"><li id="li1733223714507">测试用例脚本文件需与测试套脚本文件位于同一目录。</li><li id="li1633210375501">测试用例脚本文件的文件名前缀是“TC_”（例如：TC_Login.py）。</li></ol> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p79141439195217"><strong>方式二： </strong>在测试套配置文件中指定所有的测试用例脚本文件路径，详情请参考上文的<strong>“测试套配置文件“</strong>小节。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p19914339175218"></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul1891473911522"><li id="li18914143955210"><strong>测试用例执行</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p109149396526">本章节主要介绍测试用例的执行方式。测试用例支持两种执行方式：一是通过命令行执行，二是通过 PyCharm IDE 中的DevEco Testing Hypium 插件进行一键执行。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1291415396523"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6914163945218"><strong>命令介绍</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18914203975218">Hypium框架命令可以分为三类：help、list和run。其中run为最常用的执行命令。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p548412337615"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12915183935214"><strong>命令交互入口</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p99158398524">打开命令行窗口，切换到测试脚本工程的根目录，执行以下命令可以进入Hypium控制台。</p> <div id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p19150399522"><strong>help命令</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p39151639105211">输入help指令可以查询框架指令帮助信息。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3575175563219">help run：展示run指令相关说明；help list：展示 list指令相关说明。</p> </div></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p14916173913528"><strong>list命令</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p391663995216">list指令用来展示设备和相关的任务信息。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cangjie" class="hljs-variable">list</span> <span class="hljs-variable">history</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable">list</span> <span class="hljs-number">6</span><span class="hljs-variable">e</span>****<span class="hljs-number">90</span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18592058113312">list：展示设备信息；</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9374257344">list history：展示任务历史信息；</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p16955938123313">list&lt; id &gt;：展示特定id的任务其历史信息。</p> </div></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p391753916525"><strong>run命令</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p29181539185217">run指令主要用于执行测试任务。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-vbnet" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen5918439125217" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-symbol">run:</span></li><li>    This command <strong><span class="hljs-built_in">is</span></strong> used <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> execute the selected testcases.</li><li>    It includes a series <span class="hljs-keyword">of</span> processes such <strong><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></strong> use <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> compilation, execution, <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> result collection.  </li><li><span class="hljs-symbol">usage:</span> run [-l TESTLIST [TESTLIST ...] | -tf TESTFILE</li><li>            [TESTFILE ...]] [-tc TESTCASE] [-c CONFIG] [-sn DEVICE_SN]</li><li>            [-rp REPORT_PATH [REPORT_PATH ...]]</li><li>            [-respath RESOURCE_PATH [RESOURCE_PATH ...]]</li><li>            [-tcpath TESTCASES_PATH [TESTCASES_PATH ...]]</li><li>            [-ta TESTARGS [TESTARGS ...]]</li><li>            [-env TEST_ENVIRONMENT [TEST_ENVIRONMENT ...]]</li><li>            [--retry RETRY] [--session SESSION]</li><li>            [--repeat REPEAT]</li><li>            action task  </li><li>Specify tests <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> run.</li><li>  positional arguments:</li><li>  action                Specify action</li><li>  task                    Specify task name,such <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"ssts"</span></span>, <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"acts"</span></span>, <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"hits"</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p15919039195218">run常用指令基本使用方式如下：</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table17919239105210" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p4925539105214"><strong>PyCharm中用例执行</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1392513391522">Pycharm中执行用例依赖本文档的安装向导部分介绍的PyCharm插件：<strong> </strong>DevEco Testing Hypium，请参考本文档的<strong>“安装向导 -&gt; DevEco Testing Hypium插件安装及使用方法”</strong>小节。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p14925193916528"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p992613393526"><strong>测试报告查看</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p192683914525">测试框架执行完用例后，会生成执行结果报告。报告默认存放在测试工程目录的reports目录下。如果用户在启动测试任务时通过-rp参数指定了报告路径，报告会生成在指定的路径下。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1395653116144">测试报告目录结构如下：</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-bash" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen7926203935215" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>当前报告目录（默认目录/指定目录）</li><li>    ├── details（用例步骤截图存放目录）</li><li>    ├── result（模块执行结果存放目录）</li><li>    │     ├── &lt;测试用例1结果&gt;.xml</li><li>    │     ├──  ... ...  </li><li>    ├── <span class="hljs-built_in">log</span> (设备和任务运行<span class="hljs-built_in">log</span>存放目录)</li><li>    │     ├── &lt;测试用例1设备执行&gt;.<span class="hljs-built_in">log</span></li><li>    │     ├── ... ...</li><li>    │     ├── &lt;任务执行&gt;.<span class="hljs-built_in">log</span></li><li>    ├── static (报告展示页面css元素存放目录)</li><li>    ├── summary_report.html（测试任务可视化报告）</li><li>    ├── summary_report.xml（测试任务数据报告）</li><li>    ├── summary.ini（记录测试类型，使用的设备，开始时间和结束时间等信息）</li><li>    ├── task_info.record（记录执行命令，失败用例等清单信息）</li></ol></pre></div></div> </div> <div class="tiledSection"><h2 id="section1141818121333">API使用说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1141818121333" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5194143014215">Hypium测试框架提供了两大类API来支持用例的编写：设备相关API和设备无关API。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p064012216210">设备相关的API主要包括四个基础API类：<strong>UiDriver，BY，IUiComponent，UiWindow</strong>。</p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul20913101453811"><li id="li1791391443820"><strong>UiDriver</strong>类为UI测试的入口，代表了一个被测设备，提供控件查找、控件检查、用户操作模拟、执行shell命令、安装卸载应用等UI测试核心能力。</li><li id="li89131114133811"><strong>BY</strong>对象用于描述需要操作的控件属性，实现控件定位。</li><li id="li1891315140382"><strong>IUiComponent</strong>为UiDriver查找返回的控件对象，提供控件属性查询、控件点击、滑动查找等触控/检视能力。</li><li id="li691418147385"><strong>UiWindow</strong>为UiDriver查找返回的窗口对象，提供窗口属性查询、窗口拖动、大小调整等触控能力。</li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2079718634111"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-python" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen16610328112015" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class=""><span class="hljs-comment"># -*- coding: utf-8 -*-</span></span></li><li><span <span class=""><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> </span><span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">setup</span></span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-params">self</span></span>):</li><li>        <span class=""><span class="hljs-keyword">pass</span></span></li><li>
</li><li><span class="">    <span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> </span><span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">process</span></span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-params">self</span></span>):</li><li>        <em><span class="hljs-comment"># </span></em><em><span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">创建</span></span><span class=""><span class="hljs-string">蓝牙</span></span><span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"</span></span>))</li><li>        <em><span class="hljs-comment"># </span></em><em><span class=""><span class="hljs-comment">查找窗口</span></span></em></li><li>        <span class="">window </span>= driver.find_window(WindowFilter().bundle_name(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"com.huawei.hmos.settings"</span></span>))</li><li>    <span class=""><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> </span><span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">teardown</span></span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-params">self</span></span>):</li><li>        <span class=""><span class="hljs-keyword">pas</span></span><span class=""><span class="hljs-keyword">s</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p76646158511">设备无关的API当前主要包括两个基础API类： <strong>host</strong><span style="color: rgb(12,12,12);"> 和</span><strong>CV</strong>。</p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul1066416151354"><li id="li106640157512"><strong>host</strong> 提供基础值断言，PC端shell命令执行等PC端基础操作能力。</li><li id="li56641915953"><strong>CV</strong> 提供图像查找，图像比较，压缩，清晰度计算等基础图像操作能力。</li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p337353720"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-makefile" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen172934311267" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><strong>from</strong> hypium <strong>import</strong> host, CV</li><li>
</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 执行PC端命令</span></em></li><li>echo = host.shell(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"a.bat"</span></span>)</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 调用图像接口</span></em></li><li>brightness = CV.calculate_brightness(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"/path/to/image.jpeg"</span></span>)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p174491956170">此外Hypium还包含一些常量类型，例如<strong>KeyCode，UiParam，MatchPattern</strong>等，以及数据类型<strong>Point，Rect</strong>等。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p890118192817"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-python" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen74037544818" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><strong><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></strong> hypium.model <strong><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></strong> KeyCode, UiParam, MatchPattern</li><li>
</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 按下电源键（使用常量KeyCode.POWER）</span></em></li><li>driver.press_key(KeyCode.POWER)</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 向左滑动屏幕（使用常量UiParam.LEFT）</span></em></li><li>driver.swipe(UiParam.LEFT)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2090111191983">下文各小节将详细介绍主要测试场景中Hypium的API的使用方法。</p> <div class="tiledSection"><h2 id="section4598236435">API使用方法<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section4598236435" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2></div> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul156466714416"><li id="li9646107104120"><strong>控件查看</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p09148422618">通过 DevEco Testing Hypium插件中的 UiViewer 工具，可以查看界面控件的各项属性，有助于在后续测试用例开发中准确定位控件。具体使用方法请参考本文档的<strong>“安装向导 -&gt; DevEco Testing Hypium插件安装及使用方法</strong>“小节。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p16111191419521"><span><img originheight="931" originwidth="901" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201408.57136852970050197613525942569656:50001231000000:2800:FF3F7DBB5109F3C27AC1509FB996F283A23042892EB0B6A818E8D8B73E3C3BBF.png" title="点击放大" width="901" height="931"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6429461232"></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul718351744115"><li id="li3183191712415"><strong>控件查找</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1074617325910">Hypium 支持三种主要的控件定位方式：控件属性定位、图片匹配定位和比例坐标定位。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17150152516288">从定位的稳定性与可靠性来看，优先级如下：</p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul131500256288"><li id="li815012514285"><strong>首选：</strong>控件属性定位（基于控件的属性信息精确定位）；</li><li id="li715022510284"><strong>次选：</strong>图片匹配定位（适用于属性不可用但界面稳定的场景）；</li><li id="li21502258287"><strong>备用：</strong>比例坐标定位（仅在前两种方式不可用时使用，受分辨率影响较大）。</li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p181508251287">控件属性定位通过BY选择器对象来实现。下文将详细介绍基于控件属性、图片匹配和比例坐标三种方式的控件定位方法。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p450981031515"><strong>单属性定位控件</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5874175211145">从<strong>hypium</strong>包中导入BY选择器对象，从<strong>hypium.model</strong>包中导入匹配模式常量类<strong>MatchPattern</strong>。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-javascript" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen284285001517" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><strong><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></strong> hypium <strong><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> </strong><span class="hljs-variable constant_">BY</span></li><li><strong><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> </strong>hypium.<span class="hljs-property">model</span> <strong><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></strong> <span class="hljs-title class_">MatchPattern</span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1574185981519">通过BY对象描述需要查找或者操作的控件对象的属性，例如查找text属性为“蓝牙”的控件。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-ini" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen2677133181620" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 查找text属性为"控件文本"的控件。</span></em></li><li><span class="hljs-attr">component</span> = driver.find_component(BY.text(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"蓝牙"</span></span>))</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 读取控件的的边框位置</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-attr">bounds</span> = component.getBounds()</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 直接点击控件</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-attr">component</span> = driver.touch(BY.text(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"蓝牙"</span></span>))</li></ol></pre></div></div> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1556243311338">默认情况下，find_component和touch等方法会查找/操作第一个条件匹配的控件，如需操作第n个满足匹配条件的控件，请参考查找所有匹配控件。</p> </div></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p264715900">当前字符串类型的控件属性支持以下五种<strong>模糊匹配</strong>方式，通过BY选择器方法的第二个可选参数指定，如下表所示：</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table16411015402" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p87681568116">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="44.15%"><p </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row123446596177"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.809999999999999%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p113451359141713">5</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="44.15%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2345359201711">MatchPattern.REGEXP_ICASE</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="40.04%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13225191112217">BY.enabled</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="28.82%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p182254110214">否</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row132258117210"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3692131511219">9</p> </td> <td id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p142251811628">bool</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="22.48%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p122514111629">BY.focused</p> </td> <td id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1322517117218">selected</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="18.98%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1122519113212">bool</p> </td> <td id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row369710327169"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p36987326162">12</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="22.2%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p106989322167">hint</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="18.98%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p769818324165">str</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="22.48%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17698123231613">BY.hint</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="28.82%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p46981032111610">是</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p202401119315"><strong>多属性组合定位控件</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1031614531422">BY选择器支持链式调用，允许用户指定多个控件属性进行联合定位。当界面上存在多个控件的部分属性相同而其他属性不同时，可通过组合条件精确匹配目标控件。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-vbnet" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen8100204917310" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em># 点击文本为<span class="hljs-string">"蓝牙"</span>, 类型为<span class="hljs-string">"Button"</span>, 并且<span class="hljs-keyword">key</span>为<span class="hljs-string">"bluetooth_switch"</span>的按钮</em>。</li><li>driver.touch(<span class="hljs-keyword">BY</span>.<span
