</li><li><em># </em><em>查找</em><em>文本为<span class="hljs-string">"蓝牙"</span>, 类型为<span class="hljs-string">"Button"</span>, 并且<span class="hljs-keyword">key</span>为<span class="hljs-string">"bluetooth_switch"</span>的按钮</em>。</li><li>component = driver.find_component(<span class="hljs-keyword">BY</span>.<span class="hljs-keyword">text</span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"蓝牙"</span></span>).<span class="">type</span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"Button"</span></span>).<span class="hljs-keyword">key</span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"bluetooth_switch"</span></span>))</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6986185313517"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p075010298512"><strong>控件相对位置+属性组合定位控件</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p165010461053">对于某些自身属性不唯一，无法精确定位的控件，BY选择器支持通过<strong>与其他控件的相对位置关系</strong>来定位控件。支持的相对定位方式如下表所示：</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table20343461050" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row11501246453"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.1.4.1.1" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18103833261">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="35.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p175016461250">相对位置定位接口</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="56.589999999999996%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1050446457">功能描述</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1501346758"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p171035331567">1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="35.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1950154619510">BY.isBefore</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="56.589999999999996%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p750184611510">匹配在指定控件前边的控件。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row45024613517"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1510311333614">2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="35.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p145018462055">BY.isAfter</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="56.589999999999996%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p165034611516">匹配在指定控件后边的控件。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row65014465515"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p121032330615">3</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="35.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p105064613519">BY.within</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="56.589999999999996%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p15501346551">匹配在指定控件内部的控件。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row17500461512"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p410319331769">4</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="35.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p85074618517">BY.inWindow</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="56.589999999999996%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p850124615515">匹配在指定窗口内部的控件。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12935111013465"><strong>注意： </strong> 相对位置中的“前后”关系，对应控件树的前序遍历顺序（即深度优先遍历中根-子节点的访问次序），用户可以在 UiViewer 的可视化控件树中直观查看该顺序：控件在列表中从上到下的排列顺序，即为其在相对定位中的从前到后顺序。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p162731620144510"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13505461357">相对位置通常和控件的属性结合使用来定位控件，以下图场景为例，界面上存在多个按钮，用户需要点击显示通知图标之后的按钮，定位方式如下：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1944013241378"><span><img originheight="394" originwidth="337" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201408.74308335030140886673359167955074:50001231000000:2800:72A4795AF7EF90E407969DD7513A4B2BE773FD194F17599B3FDC296E994A7AE8.png" title="点击放大" width="337" height="394"></span></p> <ol id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ol15221041271"><li id="li72294118715">首先选择一个可以通过属性唯一定位的锚点控件。例如<strong>BY.text("显示通知图标")</strong></li><li id="li62213411475">然后找到需要操作的目标控件，选择该控件的一个不唯一属性，通常为type属性。例如<strong>BY.type("Button")</strong></li><li id="li42217411174">使用相对位置接口来描述锚点控件和目标控件的位置关系，得到完整的控件选择器。例如<strong>BY.type("Button").isAfter(BY.text</strong><strong>("显示通知图标"))</strong>，注意到这里组合使用了type属性和isAfter相对位置接口。</li></ol> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p123294471875"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-vbnet" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen528416597816" data-highlighted="yes"><ol _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-vbnet" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen44321611299" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em># 查找包名为<span class="hljs-string">"com.huawei.hmos.settings"</span>的应用内部的<span class="hljs-keyword">text</span>属性为<span class="hljs-string">"蓝牙"</span>的控件</em>。</li><li>component = driver.find_component(<span class="hljs-keyword">BY</span>.<span class=""><span class="hljs-keyword">text</span></span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"蓝牙"</span></span>).inWindow(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"com.huawei.hmos.settings"</span></span>))</li></ol></pre></div></div> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9171135418383">相对位置中的锚点控件<strong>不能</strong>再使用相对位置描述，即<strong>BY.isBefore</strong>方法的参数中不能再出现<strong>BY.isBefore</strong>或者<strong>BY.isAfter</strong>等相对定位的方式。</p> </div></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1464791216386"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p252704514123"><strong>XPath方式查找匹配的控件</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p10967101714541">BY.xpath匹配器支持通过XPath语法来查找控件。部分控件没有唯一定位的属性，同时通过相对定位的方式也无法准确定位，推荐使用XPath语法来进行更精确的控件定位。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p154965903711">XPath不能和其他属性匹配一起使用，通过XPath查找控件相比单属性和多属性查找控件的效率会有所下降。</p> </div></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p31158155510">在如下场景中，用户需要找到红框标识的图标，然而该图标没有唯一定位的属性，推荐使用XPath语法描述该控件相对其他可定位控件的路径关系来定位该控件。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p16124172471319"><span><img originheight="925" originwidth="908" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201408.87114670157546532655639138799276:50001231000000:2800:76C4310F1420319FAA7F70C9B9978D9E5F6527D5FA3B2A4AD582A8B2F108DAD7.png" title="点击放大" width="908" height="925"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p114551882215">该页面上，“可用 WLAN”是一个固定的可唯一定位的文本，用户可以首先通过XPath定位到该文本<strong>//*[@text='可用 WLAN']</strong>，然后定位到该文本控件所在的List控件<strong>/ancestor::List</strong>，然后从该List控件开始找到对应的Image控件<strong>/ListItemGroup/ListItem[1]//Text/following::Image</strong>。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p16593163691917"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-makefile" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen149771053101920" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em><span class=""><span class="hljs-comment"># 查找上图中红框所示的图标，并点击</span></span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>comp = driver.find_component(BY.xpath(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"//*[@text='可用 WLAN']/ancestor::List/ListItemGroup/ListItem[1]</span></span><span class=""><span class="hljs-string">//Text/following::Image"</span></span>))</li><li>comp.click()</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9902143081318">在支持传入BY选择器的接口均可以使用XPath来定位控件。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-perl" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen11658175414200" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 查找text属性为WLAN的控件</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.find_component(BY.xpath(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"//*[@text='WLAN']"</span></span>))</li><li>driver.find_all_components(BY.xpath(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"//*[@text='WLAN']"</span></span>))</li><li>driver.wait_for_component(BY.xpath(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"//*[@text='WLAN']"</span></span>))</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 点击text属性为WLAN的控件</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.touch(BY.xpath(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"//*[@text='WLAN']"</span></span>))</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p123091331201319"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p884021516186"><strong>查找所有匹配控件</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p151066497013">默认情况下，<strong>driver.find_component</strong>接口和其他支持传入BY选择器的接口会查找第一个匹配的控件进行操作。对于需要操作特定次序的匹配控件或所有匹配控件的场景，用户可以使用<strong>driver.find_all_components</strong>接口。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p207293503182">以如下场景为例，界面上存在多个Button，用户需要点击第2个特定的Button或点击所有Button时，可以使用<strong>driver.find_all_components</strong>。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p139041544172110"><span><img originheight="395" originwidth="343" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201408.86729051478302090546119141953826:50001231000000:2800:24FABD56F6D57916B7ECCB626E019D2E5DAE5337650E99C1DBF5B027EB6F7C72.png" title="点击放大" width="343" height="395"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6647155002118"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-bash" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen759371122210" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 查找所有type属性为"Button"的控件, 如果有匹配的结果，components为列表，包含多个满足条件的IUiComponent对象</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>components = driver.find_all_components(BY.<span class=""><span class="hljs-built_in">type</span></span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"Button"</span></span>))</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 点击所有的控件</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> component <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> components:</li><li>    driver.touch(component)</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 点击第2个控件</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.touch(component[1])</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2851116141813"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1212016132316"><strong>图片定位控件</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p77749010239">如果控件没有可用于定位的唯一属性，通过相对位置也无法实现定位，可以通过截取控件的图片，使用<strong>driver.find_image</strong>查找控件的位置，或使用<strong>driver.touch_image</strong>直接点击控件。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1777418072316">以如下场景为例，若红框中的控件没有可以唯一定位的属性，也无法通过与附近控件的相对位置定位，用户可以尝试使用图片匹配的方式定位控件，定位方式如下：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9176133519239"><span><img originheight="181" originwidth="335" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201408.69235588012243055245127453106618:50001231000000:2800:AFF03D90691D6E906919D22757B7A26D32DCB02F40BA0F96F0EFC90140C5C017.png" title="点击放大" width="335" height="181"></span></p> <ol id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ol542693782313"><li id="li19426113792310">截取红框中图片保存到为template.jpeg（文件名根据需要定义）。</li><li id="li14267376231">调用driver.touch_image，传入template.jpeg图片的路径。</li></ol> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1834812411404">使用图片定位控件需要安装opencv-python包，使用如下命令安装：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p4740151612479"><span style="color: rgb(79,129,189);">python -m pip</span> install opencv-python</p> </div></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2211182234"><strong>示例代码</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-bash" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen14424115243" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 点击屏幕上和模板图片template.jpeg匹配的位置</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.touch_image(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"/path/to/template.jpeg"</span></span>)</li><li>
</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 查找屏幕上和模板图片template.jpeg匹配的位置, bounds为Rect类型，记录了控件上下左右边框的位置</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>bounds = driver.find_image(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"template.jpeg"</span></span>)</li><li><span class=""><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span>(bounds.top, bounds.left, bounds.bottom, bounds.right)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p15481444134213">当前仅支持查找匹配度最高的匹配的图片区域，不支持匹配多个目标。</p> </div></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1882451617138"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p7989105711243"><strong>比例坐标定位控件</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p10411446546">如果图像特征不明显，使用图像匹配的方式也无法准确识别控件位置，用户可以通过比例坐标的方式点击控件。使用坐标的方式操作控件存在以下两个问题：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p845284925411">1. 在屏幕比例或者控件位置发生变化时该方法可能无法操作到预期的控件。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p26041531542">2. 当实际操作界面非预期页面时，点击也会成功，但实际执行效果不符合预期。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3478135322414">因此，在使用该方法时，建议用户在前一步或者后一步操作中通过控件属性定位控件，避免脚本未按照预期方式操作设备，但用例仍然可以执行通过的问题。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3478105392413">以下图场景为例，如果红框中的控件无法通过上述方式定位，用户可以采用比例坐标的方式点击。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1819543162010"><span><img originheight="526" originwidth="355" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201409.01225936332239277106195767465828:50001231000000:2800:84AF32661F4A4EE1D4A41A45F0C8042F6FADBCCDF115E255B813E11DA9726F53.png" title="点击放大" width="355" height="526"></span></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p166251923102410">用户可以通过 UiViewer 工具的控件查看模式获取控件的比例坐标。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9917955182511"><span><img originheight="36" originwidth="233" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120201409.86674549890317762468531699716913:50001231000000:2800:A8C0C341EDA6DA3B06E447B98E1C064FEA3236CF631F096C00CDBA614C99C4BB.png" class="notEnlarge" width="233" height="36"></span></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-bash" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen286815111262" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 点击屏幕上(0.52 * 屏幕宽度, 0.98 * 屏幕高度)的位置</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.touch((<span class=""><span class="hljs-number">0.52</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.98</span></span>))</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11241143118269"></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul119091235184118"><li id="li18909835164117"><strong>窗口查找</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p0523850202611"><strong>查找窗口</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-python" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen87681166276" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">find_window</span></span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">filter</span></span></span><span class="hljs-params">: WindowFilter</span>) -&gt; UiWindow</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p2731125142715"><strong>接口说明</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p27352512271">根据指定条件查找窗口，返回窗口对象。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1773825112711"><strong>参数说明</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table156142511272" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row17352502719"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.103.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="12.85%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1373125192716">参数名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.103.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="87.15%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9747252278">参数描述</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row27415255274"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="12.85%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3741525202714">filter</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="87.15%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13741625162710">使用WindowFilter对象指定的窗口查找条件</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1774192512719"><strong>返回值</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p274725102717">如果找到window则返回UiWindow对象，否则返回None。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17592142961315"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p57411256273"><strong>使用示例</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-ini" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen0979480283" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 查找标题为日历的窗口</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-attr">window</span> = driver.find_window(WindowFilter().title(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"日历"</span></span>))</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 查找包名为com.huawei.hmos.calendar，并且处于活动状态的窗口</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-attr">window</span> = driver.find_window(WindowFilter().bundle_name(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"com.huawei.hmos.calendar"</span></span>).actived(<span class=""><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span>))</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 查找处于活动状态的窗口</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-attr">window</span> = driver.find_window(WindowFilter().actived(<span class=""><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span>))</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 查找聚焦状态的窗口</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-attr">window</span> = driver.find_window(WindowFilter().focused(<span class=""><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span>))</li></ol></pre></div></div> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul981444444119"><li id="li128151544124119"><strong>界面操作</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3643143574017"><strong>Ⅰ.触摸屏</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12247910164112"><strong>点击</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cangjie" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen6357111915411" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><strong><span class="hljs-variable">def</span> <span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">touch</span></span></strong>(<span class="hljs-variable">target</span>: <strong style="color: rgb(79,129,189);"><span class="hljs-title class_">Union</span></strong>[<span class="hljs-title class_">ISelector</span>, <span class="hljs-variable">IUiComponent</span>, <span class=""><span class="hljs-variable">tuple</span></span>], <span class="hljs-variable">mode</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-title class_">str</span></span> = <span class="hljs-variable">UiParam</span>.<span class="hljs-variable">NORMAL</span>, <span class="hljs-variable">scroll_target</span>: <strong style="color: rgb(79,129,189);"><span class="hljs-title class_">Union</span></strong>[<span class="hljs-title class_">ISelector</span>, <span class="hljs-variable">IUiComponent</span>] = <span id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1246616122077">根据选定的控件或坐标位置执行点击操作。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1346610122078"><strong>参数说明</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table19438712971" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1146613123717"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.116.1.4.1.1" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p695010216156">1. BY控件选择器</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6670844151416">2. 控件对象</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1012173271417">2. 屏幕坐标（通过tuple类型指定，例如(100, 200)， 其中100为x轴坐标，200为y轴坐标。）</p> </td> id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p94666121474">UiParam.LONG 长按（长按后放开）</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p146613123716">UiParam.DOUBLE 双击。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1846715122716">指定可滚动的控件，在该控件中滚动搜索指定的目标控件target，仅在target为BY选择器时有效。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row246751211715"><td class="cellrowborder" 0.4)的位置。</span></em></li><li>driver.multi_finger_touch([(0.1, 0.2), (0.3, 0.4)])</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 执行多指点击操作, 设置点击按下时间为1秒。</span></em></li><li>driver.multi_finger_touch([(0.1, area=comp.getBounds())</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p19426171932419"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p114277141589"><strong>滑动</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p642814214268"><strong>执行指定方向的滑动操作</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cangjie" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen12261165116810" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><strong><span class="hljs-variable">def</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">swipe</span></strong>(<span class="hljs-variable">direction</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-title class_">str</span></span>, <span class="hljs-variable">distance</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-title class_">int</span></span> = <span class="hljs-number">60</span>, <span id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p111244571581">在屏幕上或者指定区域中执行朝向指定方向的滑动操作。该接口用于无需指定精确起始和结束坐标的滑动操作场景。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p184811708104"><strong>参数说明</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table845614020103" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row19481807101"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="12.1%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p184811108104">参数名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.145.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="80.38%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1481140191015">参数描述</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row848140151017"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11481100181012">direction</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="80.38%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p34814081019">滑动方向，目前支持：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1148112041011">UiParam.LEFT 左滑</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p44814015108">UiParam.RIGHT 右滑</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1948112061017">UiParam.UP 上滑</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p948115011106">UiParam.DOWN 下滑</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1948111014107"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p845294351013">2</p> </td> <td id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p8481150111013">相对滑动区域总长度的滑动距离，范围为1-100，表示滑动长度为滑动区域总长度的1%到100%， 默认为60。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row64812021015"><td class="cellrowborder" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1548110191016">通过控件指定的滑动区域，默认为None表示滑动区域为整个屏幕。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row134817091014"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p134818041013">side</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="80.38%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p15481170141017">滑动位置， 指定滑动区域内部（屏幕内部）执行操作的大概位置，支持：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p44813016109">UiParam.LEFT 靠左区域</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p134811408107">UiParam.RIGHT 靠右区域</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3481100181016">UiParam.TOP 靠上区域</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p04813019106">UiParam.BOTTOM 靠下区域</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1348112051012"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p24523439105">5</p> </td> <td id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p66589092012">滑动起始点，默认为None，表示在区域中间位置执行滑动操作，可以传入滑动起始点坐标，支持使用比例坐标，例如(0.5, 0.5)。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12481140111014">当同时传入side和start_point的时候，仅start_point生效。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row1148100191016"><td class="cellrowborder" </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p3419581114"><strong>使用示例</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen11186715101120" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 在屏幕上向上滑动, 距离40</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.swipe(UiParam.UP, distance=<span class="">40</span>)</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 在屏幕上向右滑动, 滑动时间为0.1秒</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.swipe(UiParam.RIGHT, swipe_time=<span class="">0.1</span>)</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 在屏幕起始点为比例坐标为(0.8, 0.8)的位置向上滑动，距离30</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.swipe(UiParam.UP, <span class="">30</span>, start_point=(<span class="">0.8, 0.8</span>))</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 在屏幕左边区域向下滑动， 距离3</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">0。</span></li><li>driver.swipe(UiParam.DOWN, <span class="">30</span>, side=UiParam.LEFT)</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 在屏幕右侧区域向上滑动，距离30</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.swipe(UiParam.UP, side=UiParam.RIGHT)</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 在类型为Scroll的控件中向上滑动</span></em><span id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5540325111212"><strong>执行指定起始结束位置的精确滑动操作</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="hljs-number">0.3</span>)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p111461715163018"><strong>接口说明</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9434101018276">根据指定的起始和结束位置执行滑动操作，起始和结束的位置可以为控件或屏幕坐标。该接口用于执行精准的滑动操作。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p185562228279"><strong>参数说明</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table252813228277" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row855618222274"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.154.1.4.1.1" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1222583711274">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.154.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="11.03%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18556722102711">参数名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.154.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="81.45%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12556122211279">参数描述</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row135561222132712"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p82252375278">1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.03%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p145565220274">start</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="81.45%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5556182292718">滑动起始位置，支持三种类型：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1641642016216">1. BY控件选择器</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p10416420192116">2. 控件对象</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p241612082110">3. 屏幕坐标（通过tuple类型指定，例如(100, 200)， 其中100为x轴坐标，200为y轴坐标。）</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row165566229276"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1822512373276">2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.03%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p15571422152715">end</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="81.45%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p4557132292715">滑动结束位置，支持三种类型：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p45191435102113">1. BY控件选择器</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1519103552115">2. 控件对象</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6519935142117">3. 屏幕坐标（通过tuple类型指定，例如(100, 200)， 其中100为x轴坐标，200为y轴坐标。）</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row255716227272"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1522583712712">3</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.03%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p125571122172718">area</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="81.45%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p7557722152715">滑动操作区域。指定区域后，当start或end参数为坐标类型时，其坐标被视为相对于该指定的区域的相对位置坐标。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row14557122272716"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p19225183762716">4</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="11.03%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1555752212279">slide_time</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="81.45%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9557222122713">滑动时间，单位为秒，默认为0.3秒。</p> id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen19401830102912" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 从类型为Slider的控件滑动到文本为最大的控件</span></em></li><li>driver.slide<span class="hljs-punctuation">(</span><span class=""><span class="hljs-number">100</span>, <span class="hljs-number">200</span></span><span class="hljs-punctuation">)</span>, <span class="hljs-punctuation">)</span></li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 从坐标100, 200滑动到300，400, 滑动时间为3秒</span></em></li><li>driver.slide<span class="hljs-punctuation">(</span><span class="hljs-punctuation">(</span><span class=""><span class="hljs-number">100</span>, <span class="hljs-number">200</span></span><span class="hljs-punctuation">)</span>, <span 0)滑动到(100, 0)</span></em></li><li>driver.slide<span class="hljs-punctuation">(</span><span class="hljs-punctuation">(</span><span class=""><span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span class="hljs-punctuation">)</span>, <span class="hljs-punctuation">(</span><span class=""><span class="hljs-number">100</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span class="hljs-punctuation">)</span>, area <span class="hljs-punctuation">=</span> BY.<span class="hljs-keyword">type</span><span class="hljs-punctuation">)</span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p47732093293"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1223763113119"><strong>拖拽</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cangjie" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen11702636101210" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><strong><span class="hljs-variable">def</span> <span class=""><span class="hljs-title id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p8420144431215"><strong>接口说明</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13420194413129">根据指定的起始和结束位置执行拖拽操作，起始和结束的位置可以为控件或者屏幕坐标。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1170985417125"><strong>参数说明</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table768405417129" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row670975416129"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.163.1.4.1.1" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p4231592132">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.163.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="15.590000000000002%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p97091954201214">参数名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.163.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="76.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18709354171217">参数描述</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row9709135461219"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p172316951319">1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.590000000000002%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p270910549124">start</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="76.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p87092546128">拖拽起始位置，支持三种类型：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1288684362516">1. BY控件选择器</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p4886743182510">2. 控件对象</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5886194352512">3. 屏幕坐标（通过tuple类型指定的坐标，例如(100, 200)， 其中100为x轴坐标，200为y轴坐标；或相对于区域长度和宽度的比例坐标，例如(0.1, 0.2)。)</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row4709195471214"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p152313917134">2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.590000000000002%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p20709754181213">end</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="76.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17099546127">拖拽结束位置，支持三种类型：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1921135052514">1. BY控件选择器</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p82111150112514">2. 控件对象</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6211350192514">3. 屏幕坐标（通过tuple类型指定的坐标，例如(100, 200)， 其中100为x轴坐标，200为y轴坐标；或相对于区域长度和宽度的比例坐标，例如(0.1, 0.2)。)</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row7709154181217"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13238981311">3</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.590000000000002%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1570915418124">area</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="76.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18709185411215">拖拽操作区域，指定区域后，当start或end参数为坐标类型时，其坐标被视为相对于该指定的区域的相对位置坐标。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row15709145431214"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9248981314">4</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.590000000000002%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p47090548121">press_time</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="76.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p56311659154317">拖拽操作开始时，长按的时间，单位为秒，默认为1.5秒。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p181311111447"><strong>注意：</strong> 该参数为可选参数，仅DevEco Testing Hypium 6.0.5.200及更新的版本，且配套测试设备的API level &gt;= 20时支持。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row14709155411121"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18248912131">5</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="15.590000000000002%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p77091554101220">drag_time</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="76.89%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18709115481216">拖动的时间，单位秒， 默认为1秒（拖拽操作总时间 = press_time + drag_time）。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p8196358171319"><strong>捏合缩小</strong></p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cangjie" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen1577310803220" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><strong><span class="hljs-variable">def</span> <span class=""><span class="hljs-title function_">pinch_in</span></span></strong>(<span class="hljs-variable">area</span>: <strong><span class=""><span class="hljs-title class_">Union</span></span></strong>[<span class="hljs-title class_">ISelector</span>, <span class="hljs-variable">IUiComponent</span>, <span class="hljs-variable">Rect</span>], <span class="hljs-variable">scale</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-title class_">float</span></span> = <span class=""><span class="hljs-number">0.4</span></span>, <span class="hljs-variable">direction</span>: <span class=""><span class="hljs-title class_">str</span></span> = <span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"diagonal"</span></span>, **<span class="hljs-variable">kwargs</span>)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17170182773215"><strong>接口说明</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18725173717325">在指定控件上执行双指捏合缩小操作。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12613182113216"><strong>参数说明</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table145871214328" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row17613172193213"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.172.1.4.1.1" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p018613743315">序号</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.172.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="12.41%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p7614721183219">参数名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.172.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="80.07%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p461462114322">参数描述</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row13614192123213"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p21868763318">1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="12.41%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p161414211324">area</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="80.07%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1861412193217">手势操作执行的区域，支持三种类型：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6967141972813">1. BY控件选择器</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1796751919280">2. 控件对象</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p69671919122815">3. 屏幕区域，通过Rect类型指定，例如 Rect(left, right, top, bottom)，其中 left，right，top，bottom 为区域左右上下的坐标值。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row2614112117327"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p61861378331">2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="12.41%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p161412118329">scale</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="80.07%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p16614122173215">缩放的比例，范围(0, 1)，值越小表示缩放操作距离越长，缩小的越多。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row861415218324"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p018612719339">3</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="12.41%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p46141121143217">direction</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="80.07%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1661418216321">双指缩放时缩放操作方向，当前支持：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1614121173219">"diagonal" 对角线滑动</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p861492112320">"horizontal" 水平滑动</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row061422113218"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p51861973336">4</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="12.41%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p20614192183217">kwargs</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="80.07%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12614162123211">其他可选滑动配置参数：</p> <p </li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 创建一个gesture对象</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>gesture = Gesture()</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 获取控件计算器的位置</span></em><span 获取屏幕尺寸。</span></li><li>size = driver.getDisplaySize()</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 起始位置, 长按2秒</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>gesture.start(pos.to_tuple(), <span class="">int</span>(size.Y /<span class=""> 2</span>)).to_tuple())</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 停留2秒</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>gesture.pause(<span class="">2</span>)</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 移动到(360, 500)的位置</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>gesture.move_to(Point(<span class="">360, 500</span>).to_tuple())</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 停留2秒结束</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>gesture.pause(<span class="">2</span>)</li><li><em><span class="hljs-comment"># 执行gesture对象描述的操作</span></em><span class="hljs-comment">。</span></li><li>driver.inject_gesture(gesture)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__screen74461919112917" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class=""><span class="hljs-variable">def</span> </span><span class=""><span id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p20375143316297">向指定控件中输入文本内容。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p10375103310290"><strong>参数说明</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div width="16.74%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p63754333295">参数名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.370.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="75.74%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p63758339296">参数描述</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row337511338295"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p115524166521">1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="16.74%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p43756335298">component</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="75.74%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p7781162116512">需要输入文本的控件，支持三种类型：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1778017211255">1. BY控件选择器</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p178022113511">2. 控件对象</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p127806211453">3. 屏幕坐标（通过tuple类型指定，例如(100, 200)， 其中100为x轴坐标，200为y轴坐标。）</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row0375193317291"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p255231612524">2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="16.74%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17375833172911">text</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="75.74%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p53753338293">需要输入的文本。</p> </td> </tr> <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row173111423134215"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="7.5200000000000005%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11311162314212">3.</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="16.74%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p4311182316428">mode</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="75.74%"><p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1755611214379">输入模式配置，默认模式操作如下：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1250313564431">1. 默认清空指定的控件中的文本后再执行输入。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1850345611431">2. 英文字符长度&lt;200时，逐个输入，超过200时，通过剪切板粘贴一次输入。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p195031556124318">3. 中文文本通过剪切板粘贴一次输入。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p95031156144319">通过该参数可以配置：</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p7503175616436">1. 追加输入：InputTextMode().addition(True)。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p11503165614437">2. 输入英文时，不考虑文本长度直接使用剪切板快速输入：InputTextMode().paste(True)。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1047562823717"><strong>注意</strong>：该参数为可选参数，仅DevEco Testing Hypium 6.0.5.200以及更新的版本，且配套测试设备的API level &gt;= 20支持。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p279415546312">检查实际值和期望值相等，在不一致时抛出异常，并打印fail_msg。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1279413545317"><strong>参数说明</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table id="table11744195453110" class="layoutFixed idpTab"><thead><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__row19794195493116"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.390.1.4.1.1" <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul414510201599"><li id="li3145182010595"><strong>日志打印</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p625116208504">用户使用以下方法可以在测试用例脚本中打印日志，日志会记录到测试报告中。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div MESSAGE</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-built_in">Step</span>(<span class="">"点击按钮"</span>)</li><li><span class="hljs-built_in">CheckPoint</span>(<span class="">"检查联系人存在"</span>)</li><li><span class="hljs-built_in">MESSAGE</span>(<span class="">"打印一条提示消息"</span>)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p123099283501">在自定义实现的接口中，可以调用driver对象中的log模块打印日志消息，对应日志也会记录到测试报告中。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="hljs-string">"info级别的日志"</span></span>)</li><li>driver.<span class="hljs-built_in">log</span>.warning(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"warning级别的日志"</span></span>)</li><li>driver.<span class="hljs-built_in">log</span>.<span class="hljs-built_in">error</span>(<span class=""><span class="hljs-string">"error级别的日志"</span></span>)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p107541933191615"></p> <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__ul6683202865912"><li id="li768392875913"><strong>读取测试项目中资源文件路径</strong></li></ul> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p71502327574">用户可通过以下接口读取测试工程资源目录中的文件路径。接口接收文件名或相对路径作为参数，搜索测试工程资源文件目录并返回文件的完整路径。若未找到对应文件，则抛出异常。</p> <div _ngcontent-wmo-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div <div class="tiledSection"><h2 id="section112896130577">隐私协议<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section112896130577" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2></div> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5952832163718"><strong>概述</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p8952193243720">DevEco Testing Hypium(以下简称Hypium)是由华为终端有限公司（以下简称“我们”或“华为”）提供的UI自动化测试框架。华为非常重视您的个人信息和隐私保护，我们将会按照法律要求和业界成熟的安全标准，为您的个人信息提供相应的安全保护措施。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1595203218374"><strong>1 </strong><strong>我们如何收集和使用您的个人信息</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p795215321373">我们将通过Hypium为您提供下述业务功能，在您使用相关业务功能的过程中，我们会处理下列提供功能所必需的信息，以便履行我们的合同义务。若您不提供相关信息，会影响到您使用本应用的相关功能。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1995219323375"><strong>运行Hypium</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1995217328379">在您使用Hypium的过程中，我们会收集执行设备的操作系统平台和版本号，用于更好的提供和执行平台适配的测试服务。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p139521632123713"><strong>测试鸿蒙设备</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p13952832153713">当您使用Hypium测试鸿蒙设备上的应用时，我们会收集被测设备的型号以及鸿蒙系统版本、被测应用的名称或者包名、Hypium特性功能的触发时间和使用次数，用于分析Hypium各功能在不同平台上的使用情况，从而针对性的优化我们的产品，更好的为客户提供服务。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p14952153223719"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1195253203717"><strong>2 </strong><strong>对未成年人的保护</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1395263283713">我们非常重视对未成年人个人信息的保护，华为将严格按照国家法律法规要求在未成年人使用服务时提供相应的保护。如果您是未成年人，需要您的父母或其他监护人同意您使用本应用并同意相关应用的服务条款。父母或其他监护人也应采取适当的预防措施来保护未成年人，包括监督其对本应用的使用。如您是儿童，请务必退出使用本应用。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p89521032173714"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p19952193263716"><strong>3 </strong><strong>管理您的个人信息</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p12952932183712">华为非常尊重您对个人信息的关注，并为您提供了数据主体权利及选择。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p795213233719"><strong>3.1 </strong><strong>信息访问</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1095213263712">如您希望收集和存储的您的个人信息及其副本，可通过本声明中“如何联系我们”章节中所述方式与我们取得联系，并获取您的个人信息及其副本。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p18952732103710"><strong>3.2 </strong><strong>信息更正</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1895213233719">当您需要更新您的个人信息，或发现我们处理您的个人信息有误时，您有权作出更正或更新。您可以通过本声明中“如何联系我们”章节中所述方式与我们取得联系，并修改您的个人信息。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1395253263714"><strong>3.3 </strong><strong>信息删除</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p5952732113713">您随时可以通过本声明中“如何联系我们”章节中所述方式与我们取得联系，并要求我们删除您的个人信息。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p29521832173717"><strong>3.4 </strong><strong>停用服务</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p199531432153714">对于hypium-driver-js安装包，您可以在项目根目录运行 `npx hypium-driver telemetry disable` 来停止Hypium处理您的个人信息。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p795383243713">对于hypium安装包，您可以在项目根目录运行 `python -m hypium telemetry disable` 来停止Hypium处理您的个人信息。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p20953153214371">对于hypium-pycharm-plugin的插件，您可以在pycharm顶部导航栏中的DevEco Testing Hypium &gt; 隐私协议页面，点击“拒绝并关闭”按钮来停止Hypium处理您的个人信息。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p8953113218373"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p17953123216377">对于hypium-driver-js安装包，您可以在项目根目录运行 `npx hypium-driver telemetry enable ` 来恢复Hypium对您个人信息的处理。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p14953193223710">对于hypium安装包，您可以在项目根目录运行 ` python -m hypium telemetry enable` 来恢复Hypium对您个人信息的处理。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p9953193223717">对于hypium-pycharm-plugin的插件，您可以在pycharm顶部导航栏中的DevEco Testing Hypium &gt; 隐私协议页面，点击“同意并开启”按钮来恢复Hypium对您个人信息的处理。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p795343213374"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p195316329379">对于hypium-driver-js安装包，您可以在项目根目录运行 `npx hypium-driver telemetry status` 来查看Hypium个人信息处理状态。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p209531732123717">对于hypium安装包，您可以在项目根目录运行 `python -m hypium telemetry status` 来查看Hypium个人信息处理状态。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p695314324371">对于hypium-pycharm-plugin的插件，您可以在pycharm顶部导航栏中的DevEco Testing Hypium &gt; 隐私协议页面来查看Hypium个人信息处理状态。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p59538328376"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p19953123243714"><strong>4 </strong><strong>数据存储地点及期限</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p6953113211371"><strong>4.1 </strong><strong>存储地点</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p109531321377">上述信息将会传输并保存至中华人民共和国境内的服务器。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p89539328379"><strong>4.2 </strong><strong>存储期限</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p16953153210376">我们仅在实现本声明所述目的所必需的时间内保留您的个人信息，并在超出下述保留时间后删除或匿名化处理您的个人信息，除非法律法规另有要求。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1695333253714">工具自身的测试数据及其备份数据将保存5年，目的是为了确保您的数据安全。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1895313215375">此外，当我们的产品或服务发生停止运营的情形时，我们将以推送通知、公告等形式通知您，并在合理的期限内删除您的个人信息或进行匿名化处理。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p10953232103718"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1195314322375"><strong>5 </strong><strong>如何联系我们</strong></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p695353263712">我们指定了个人信息保护负责人，您可以通过此<a href="https://consumer.huawei.com/cn/legal/privacy-questions/" target="_blank">链接</a>联系个人信息保护负责人。您也可以通过访问<a href="https://consumer.huawei.com/cn/legal/privacy-questions/" target="_blank">隐私问题页面</a>与我们其取得联系，我们会尽快回复。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p159531532123716"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p14953173213720">如果您对我们的回复不满意，特别是当我们的个人信息处理行为损害了您的合法权益时，您还可以通过向有管辖权的人民法院提起诉讼、向行业自律协会或政府相关管理机构投诉等外部途径进行解决。您也可以向我们了解可能适用的相关投诉途径的信息。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p15953432173717"></p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p1095393253711">华为将始终遵照我们的隐私政策来收集和使用您的信息。有关我们的隐私政策，可参阅<a href="https://consumer.huawei.com/minisite/legal/privacy/statement.htm?code=CN&amp;language=zh-CN" target="_blank">华为消费者业务隐私声明</a>。</p> <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002506106493__p137463360377"></p> </div> <div></div></div>
